\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ stb\_image\_write\ -\/\ v1.14\ -\/\ public\ domain\ -\/\ http://nothings.org/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ writes\ out\ PNG/BMP/TGA/JPEG/HDR\ images\ to\ C\ stdio\ -\/\ Sean\ Barrett\ 2010-\/2015}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ no\ warranty\ implied;\ use\ at\ your\ own\ risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Before\ \#including,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STB\_IMAGE\_WRITE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ in\ the\ file\ that\ you\ want\ to\ have\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Will\ probably\ not\ work\ correctly\ with\ strict-\/aliasing\ optimizations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{ABOUT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ This\ header\ file\ is\ a\ library\ for\ writing\ images\ to\ C\ stdio\ or\ a\ callback.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ The\ PNG\ output\ is\ not\ optimal;\ it\ is\ 20-\/50\%\ larger\ than\ the\ file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ written\ by\ a\ decent\ optimizing\ implementation;\ though\ providing\ a\ custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ zlib\ compress\ function\ (see\ STBIW\_ZLIB\_COMPRESS)\ can\ mitigate\ that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ This\ library\ is\ designed\ for\ source\ code\ compactness\ and\ simplicity,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ not\ optimal\ image\ file\ size\ or\ run-\/time\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{BUILDING:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ \#define\ STBIW\_ASSERT(x)\ before\ the\ \#include\ to\ avoid\ using\ assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ \#define\ STBIW\_MALLOC(),\ STBIW\_REALLOC(),\ and\ STBIW\_FREE()\ to\ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ malloc,realloc,free.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ \#define\ STBIW\_MEMMOVE()\ to\ replace\ memmove()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ \#define\ STBIW\_ZLIB\_COMPRESS\ to\ use\ a\ custom\ zlib-\/style\ compress\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ for\ PNG\ compression\ (instead\ of\ the\ builtin\ one),\ it\ must\ have\ the\ following\ signature:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ unsigned\ char\ *\ my\_compress(unsigned\ char\ *data,\ int\ data\_len,\ int\ *out\_len,\ int\ quality);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ The\ returned\ data\ will\ be\ freed\ with\ STBIW\_FREE()\ (free()\ by\ default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ so\ it\ must\ be\ heap\ allocated\ with\ STBIW\_MALLOC()\ (malloc()\ by\ default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ If\ compiling\ for\ Windows\ and\ you\ wish\ to\ use\ Unicode\ filenames,\ compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBIW\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ and\ pass\ utf8-\/encoded\ filenames.\ Call\ stbiw\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8\ to\ convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Windows\ wchar\_t\ filenames\ to\ utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{USAGE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ There\ are\ five\ functions,\ one\ for\ each\ image\ file\ format:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_png(char\ const\ *filename,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ *data,\ int\ stride\_in\_bytes);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_bmp(char\ const\ *filename,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_tga(char\ const\ *filename,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_jpg(char\ const\ *filename,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ *data,\ int\ quality);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_hdr(char\ const\ *filename,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ float\ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ void\ stbi\_flip\_vertically\_on\_write(int\ flag);\ //\ flag\ is\ non-\/zero\ to\ flip\ data\ vertically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ There\ are\ also\ five\ equivalent\ functions\ that\ use\ an\ arbitrary\ write\ function.\ You\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ expected\ to\ open/close\ your\ file-\/equivalent\ before\ and\ after\ calling\ these:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_png\_to\_func(stbi\_write\_func\ *func,\ void\ *context,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ \ *data,\ int\ stride\_in\_bytes);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_bmp\_to\_func(stbi\_write\_func\ *func,\ void\ *context,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ \ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_tga\_to\_func(stbi\_write\_func\ *func,\ void\ *context,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ \ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_hdr\_to\_func(stbi\_write\_func\ *func,\ void\ *context,\ int\ w,\ int\ h,\ int\ comp,\ const\ float\ *data);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_jpg\_to\_func(stbi\_write\_func\ *func,\ void\ *context,\ int\ x,\ int\ y,\ int\ comp,\ const\ void\ *data,\ int\ quality);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ where\ the\ callback\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ void\ stbi\_write\_func(void\ *context,\ void\ *data,\ int\ size);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ configure\ it\ with\ these\ global\ variables:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_tga\_with\_rle;\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ defaults\ to\ true;\ set\ to\ 0\ to\ disable\ RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_png\_compression\_level;\ \ \ \ //\ defaults\ to\ 8;\ set\ to\ higher\ for\ more\ compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ int\ stbi\_write\_force\_png\_filter;\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ defaults\ to\ -\/1;\ set\ to\ 0..5\ to\ force\ a\ filter\ mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ You\ can\ define\ STBI\_WRITE\_NO\_STDIO\ to\ disable\ the\ file\ variant\ of\ these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ functions,\ so\ the\ library\ will\ not\ use\ stdio.h\ at\ all.\ However,\ this\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ also\ disable\ HDR\ writing,\ because\ it\ requires\ stdio\ for\ formatted\ output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Each\ function\ returns\ 0\ on\ failure\ and\ non-\/0\ on\ success.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ The\ functions\ create\ an\ image\ file\ defined\ by\ the\ parameters.\ The\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ is\ a\ rectangle\ of\ pixels\ stored\ from\ left-\/to-\/right,\ top-\/to-\/bottom.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Each\ pixel\ contains\ 'comp'\ channels\ of\ data\ stored\ interleaved\ with\ 8-\/bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ per\ channel,\ in\ the\ following\ order:\ 1=Y,\ 2=YA,\ 3=RGB,\ 4=RGBA.\ (Y\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ monochrome\ color.)\ The\ rectangle\ is\ 'w'\ pixels\ wide\ and\ 'h'\ pixels\ tall.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ The\ *data\ pointer\ points\ to\ the\ first\ byte\ of\ the\ top-\/left-\/most\ pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ For\ PNG,\ "{}stride\_in\_bytes"{}\ is\ the\ distance\ in\ bytes\ from\ the\ first\ byte\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ a\ row\ of\ pixels\ to\ the\ first\ byte\ of\ the\ next\ row\ of\ pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ PNG\ creates\ output\ files\ with\ the\ same\ number\ of\ components\ as\ the\ input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ The\ BMP\ format\ expands\ Y\ to\ RGB\ in\ the\ file\ format\ and\ does\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ output\ alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ PNG\ supports\ writing\ rectangles\ of\ data\ even\ when\ the\ bytes\ storing\ rows\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ data\ are\ not\ consecutive\ in\ memory\ (e.g.\ sub-\/rectangles\ of\ a\ larger\ image),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ by\ supplying\ the\ stride\ between\ the\ beginning\ of\ adjacent\ rows.\ The\ other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ formats\ do\ not.\ (Thus\ you\ cannot\ write\ a\ native-\/format\ BMP\ through\ the\ BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ writer,\ both\ because\ it\ is\ in\ BGR\ order\ and\ because\ it\ may\ have\ padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ at\ the\ end\ of\ the\ line.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ PNG\ allows\ you\ to\ set\ the\ deflate\ compression\ level\ by\ setting\ the\ global}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ variable\ 'stbi\_write\_png\_compression\_level'\ (it\ defaults\ to\ 8).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ HDR\ expects\ linear\ float\ data.\ Since\ the\ format\ is\ always\ 32-\/bit\ rgb(e)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ data,\ alpha\ (if\ provided)\ is\ discarded,\ and\ for\ monochrome\ data\ it\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ replicated\ across\ all\ three\ channels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ TGA\ supports\ RLE\ or\ non-\/RLE\ compressed\ data.\ To\ use\ non-\/RLE-\/compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ data,\ set\ the\ global\ variable\ 'stbi\_write\_tga\_with\_rle'\ to\ 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ JPEG\ does\ ignore\ alpha\ channels\ in\ input\ data;\ quality\ is\ between\ 1\ and\ 100.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Higher\ quality\ looks\ better\ but\ results\ in\ a\ bigger\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ JPEG\ baseline\ (no\ JPEG\ progressive).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{CREDITS:}}
